<s> and he set off running with the rest of the crowd in the direction of the fireworks <\s>
<s> so did pen presently when this agreeable youth was out of sight begin to run with his little companion mrs <\s>
<s> bolton following after them with captain costigan at her side <\s>
<s> but the captain was too majestic and dignified in his movements to run for friend or enemy and he pursued his course with the usual jaunty swagger which distinguished his steps so that he and his companion were speedily distanced by pen and miss fanny <\s>
<s> perhaps arthur forgot or perhaps he did not choose to remember that the elder couple had no money in their pockets as had been proved by their adventure at the entrance of the gardens howbeit pen paid a couple of shillings for himself and his partner and with her hanging close on his arm scaled the staircase which leads to the firework gallery <\s>
<s> the captain and mamma might have followed them if they liked but arthur and fanny were too busy to look back <\s>
<s> people were pushing and squeezing there beside and behind them <\s>
<s> one eager individual rushed by fanny and elbowed her so that she fell back with a little cry upon which of course arthur caught her adroitly in his arms and just for protection kept her so defended until they mounted the stair and took their places <\s>
<s> poor foker sate alone on one of the highest benches his face illuminated by the fireworks or in their absence by the moon <\s>
<s> arthur saw him and laughed but did not occupy himself about his friend much <\s>
<s> he was engaged with fanny <\s>
<s> how happy she was <\s>
<s> how she cried o o o as the rockets soared into the air and showered down in azure and emerald and vermilion <\s>
<s> as these wonders blazed and disappeared before her the little girl thrilled and trembled with delight at arthur's side her hand was under his arm still he felt it pressing him as she looked up delighted <\s>
<s> how beautiful they are sir <\s>
<s> don't call me sir fanny arthur said <\s>
<s> a quick blush rushed up into the girl's face <\s>
<s> what shall i call you <\s>
<s> she said in a low voice sweet and tremulous <\s>
<s> what would you wish me to say sir <\s>
<s> well i forgot it is best so my dear pendennis said very kindly and gently <\s>
<s> i may call you fanny <\s>
<s> she said and the little hand pressed his arm once more very eagerly and the girl clung to him so that he could feel her heart beating on his shoulder <\s>
<s> i may call you fanny because you are a young girl and a good girl fanny and i am an old gentleman <\s>
<s> but you mustn't call me anything but sir or mr <\s>
<s> pendennis if you like for we live in very different stations fanny and don't think i speak unkindly and and why do you take your hand away fanny <\s>
<s> are you afraid of me <\s>
<s> do you think i would hurt you <\s>
<s> not for all the world my dear little girl <\s>
<s> and and look how beautiful the moon and stars are and how calmly they shine when the rockets have gone out and the noisy wheels have done hissing and blazing <\s>
<s> when i came here to night i did not think i should have had such a pretty little companion to sit by my side and see these fine fireworks <\s>
<s> you must know i live by myself and work very hard <\s>
<s> i write in books and newspapers fanny and i quite tired out and was expected to sit alone all night and don't cry my dear dear little girl <\s>
<s> here pen broke out rapidly putting an end to the calm oration which he had begun to deliver for the sight of a woman's tears always put his nerves in a quiver and he began forthwith to coax her and soothe her and to utter a hundred and twenty little ejaculations of pity and sympathy which need not be repeated here because they would be absurd in print <\s>
<s> so would a mother's talk to a child be absurd in print so would a lover's to his bride <\s>
<s> that sweet artless poetry bears no translation and is too subtle for grammarians clumsy definitions <\s>
<s> you have but the same four letters to describe the salute which you perform on your grandmother's forehead and that which you bestow on the sacred cheek of your mistress but the same four letters and not one of them a labial <\s>
<s> do we mean to hint that r <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis made any use of the monosyllable in question <\s>
<s> in the first place it was dark the fireworks were over and nobody could see him secondly he was not a man to have this kind of secret and tell it thirdly and lastly let the honest fellow who has kissed a pretty girl say what would have been his own conduct in such a delicate juncture <\s>
<s> well the truth is that however you may suspect him and whatever you would have done under the circumstances or mr <\s>
<s> pen would have liked to do he behaved honestly and like a man <\s>
<s> i will not play with this little girl's heart he said within himself and forget my own or her honour <\s>
<s> she seems to have a great deal of dangerous and rather contagious sensibility and i am very glad the fireworks are over and that i can take her back to her mother <\s>
<s> come along fanny mind the steps and lean on me <\s>
<s> don't stumble you heedless little thing this is the way and there is your mamma at the door <\s>
<s> and there indeed mrs <\s>
<s> bolton was unquiet in spirit and grasping her umbrella <\s>
<s> she seized fanny with maternal fierceness and eagerness and uttered some rapid abuse to the girl in an undertone <\s>
<s> the expression in captain costigan's eye standing behind the matron and winking at pendennis from under his hat was i am bound to say indefinably humorous <\s>
<s> it was so much so that pen could not refrain from bursting into a laugh <\s>
<s> you should have taken my arm mrs <\s>
<s> bolton he said offering it <\s>
<s> i am very glad to bring miss fanny back quite safe to you <\s>
<s> we thought you would have followed us up into the gallery <\s>
<s> we enjoyed the fireworks didn't we <\s>
<s> said miss fanny with rather a demure look <\s>
<s> and the bouquet was magnificent said pen <\s>
<s> and it is ten hours since i had anything to eat ladies and i wish you would permit me to invite you to supper <\s>
<s> dad said costigan i'd loike a snack to only i forgawt me purse or i should have invoited these leedies to a collection <\s>
<s> bolton with considerable asperity said she ad an eadache and would much rather go ome <\s>
<s> a lobster salad is the best thing in the world for a headache pen said gallantly and a glass of wine i'm sure will do you good <\s>
<s> bolton be kind to me and oblige me <\s>
<s> i shan't have the heart to sup without you and upon my word i have had no dinner <\s>

<s> costigan i'm sure you'll take care of miss fanny and i shall think mrs <\s>
<s> bolton angry with me unless she will favour me with her society <\s>
<s> and we will all sup quietly and go back in a cab together <\s>
<s> the cab the lobster salad the frank and good humoured look of pendennis as he smilingly invited the worthy matron subdued her suspicions and her anger <\s>
<s> since he would be so obliging she thought she could take a little bit of lobster and so they all marched away to a box and costigan called for a waither with such a loud and belligerent voice as caused one of those officials instantly to run to him <\s>
<s> the carte was examined on the wall and fanny was asked to choose her favourite dish upon which the young creature said she was fond of lobster too but also owned to a partiality for raspberry tart <\s>
<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>
<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>
<s> when the supper which was very brisk and gay was over and captain costigan and mrs <\s>
<s> bolton had partaken of some of the rack punch that is so fragrant at vauxhall the bill was called and discharged by pen with great generosity loike a foin young english gentleman of th olden toime be jove costigan enthusiastically remarked <\s>
<s> and as when they went out of the box he stepped forward and gave mrs <\s>
<s> bolton his arm fanny fell to pen's lot and the young people walked away in high good humour together in the wake of their seniors <\s>
<s> the champagne and the rack punch though taken in moderation by all persons except perhaps poor cos who lurched ever so little in his gait had set them in high spirits and good humour so that fanny began to skip and move her brisk little feet in time to the band which was playing waltzes and galops for the dancers <\s>
<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>
<s> shouldn't you like a turn <\s>
<s> said the prince of fairoaks <\s>
<s> what fun it would be <\s>
<s> bolton ma'am do let me take her once round <\s>
<s> costigan said off wid you <\s>
<s> bolton not refusing indeed she was an old war horse and would have liked at the trumpet's sound to have entered the arena herself fanny's shawl was off her back in a minute and she and arthur were whirling round in a waltz in the midst of a great deal of queer but exceedingly joyful company <\s>
<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>

<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>

<s> the cab the lobster salad the frank and good humoured look of pendennis as he smilingly invited the worthy matron subdued her suspicions and her anger <\s>
<s> since he would be so obliging she thought she could take a little bit of lobster and so they all marched away to a box and costigan called for a waither with such a loud and belligerent voice as caused one of those officials instantly to run to him <\s>
<s> the carte was examined on the wall and fanny was asked to choose her favourite dish upon which the young creature said she was fond of lobster too but also owned to a partiality for raspberry tart <\s>
<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>
<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>
<s> when the supper which was very brisk and gay was over and captain costigan and mrs <\s>
<s> bolton had partaken of some of the rack punch that is so fragrant at vauxhall the bill was called and discharged by pen with great generosity loike a foin young english gentleman of th olden toime be jove costigan enthusiastically remarked <\s>
<s> and as when they went out of the box he stepped forward and gave mrs <\s>
<s> bolton his arm fanny fell to pen's lot and the young people walked away in high good humour together in the wake of their seniors <\s>
<s> the champagne and the rack punch though taken in moderation by all persons except perhaps poor cos who lurched ever so little in his gait had set them in high spirits and good humour so that fanny began to skip and move her brisk little feet in time to the band which was playing waltzes and galops for the dancers <\s>
<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>
<s> shouldn't you like a turn <\s>
<s> said the prince of fairoaks <\s>
<s> what fun it would be <\s>

<s> costigan said off wid you <\s>
<s> bolton not refusing indeed she was an old war horse and would have liked at the trumpet's sound to have entered the arena herself fanny's shawl was off her back in a minute and she and arthur were whirling round in a waltz in the midst of a great deal of queer but exceedingly joyful company <\s>
<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>
<s> huxter and his pink satin young friend of whom we have already had a glimpse <\s>
<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>
<s> the young surgeon roared out using at the same time other expressions far more emphatic and was joined in his abuse by the shrill language and laughter of his partner to the interruption of the ball the terror of poor little fanny and the immense indignation of pen <\s>

<s> a battle with a fellow like that <\s>

<s> bolton following after them with captain costigan at her side <\s>
<s> but the captain was too majestic and dignified in his movements to run for friend or enemy and he pursued his course with the usual jaunty swagger which distinguished his steps so that he and his companion were speedily distanced by pen and miss fanny <\s>
<s> perhaps arthur forgot or perhaps he did not choose to remember that the elder couple had no money in their pockets as had been proved by their adventure at the entrance of the gardens howbeit pen paid a couple of shillings for himself and his partner and with her hanging close on his arm scaled the staircase which leads to the firework gallery <\s>
<s> the captain and mamma might have followed them if they liked but arthur and fanny were too busy to look back <\s>
<s> people were pushing and squeezing there beside and behind them <\s>
<s> one eager individual rushed by fanny and elbowed her so that she fell back with a little cry upon which of course arthur caught her adroitly in his arms and just for protection kept her so defended until they mounted the stair and took their places <\s>
<s> poor foker sate alone on one of the highest benches his face illuminated by the fireworks or in their absence by the moon <\s>
<s> arthur saw him and laughed but did not occupy himself about his friend much <\s>

<s> here pen broke out rapidly putting an end to the calm oration which he had begun to deliver for the sight of a woman's tears always put his nerves in a quiver and he began forthwith to coax her and soothe her and to utter a hundred and twenty little ejaculations of pity and sympathy which need not be repeated here because they would be absurd in print <\s>

<s> the cab the lobster salad the frank and good humoured look of pendennis as he smilingly invited the worthy matron subdued her suspicions and her anger <\s>
<s> since he would be so obliging she thought she could take a little bit of lobster and so they all marched away to a box and costigan called for a waither with such a loud and belligerent voice as caused one of those officials instantly to run to him <\s>
<s> the carte was examined on the wall and fanny was asked to choose her favourite dish upon which the young creature said she was fond of lobster too but also owned to a partiality for raspberry tart <\s>
<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>
<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>
<s> when the supper which was very brisk and gay was over and captain costigan and mrs <\s>
<s> bolton had partaken of some of the rack punch that is so fragrant at vauxhall the bill was called and discharged by pen with great generosity loike a foin young english gentleman of th olden toime be jove costigan enthusiastically remarked <\s>
<s> and as when they went out of the box he stepped forward and gave mrs <\s>
<s> bolton his arm fanny fell to pen's lot and the young people walked away in high good humour together in the wake of their seniors <\s>
<s> the champagne and the rack punch though taken in moderation by all persons except perhaps poor cos who lurched ever so little in his gait had set them in high spirits and good humour so that fanny began to skip and move her brisk little feet in time to the band which was playing waltzes and galops for the dancers <\s>
<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>
<s> shouldn't you like a turn <\s>

<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>
<s> huxter and his pink satin young friend of whom we have already had a glimpse <\s>
<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>

<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>
<s> when the supper which was very brisk and gay was over and captain costigan and mrs <\s>
<s> bolton had partaken of some of the rack punch that is so fragrant at vauxhall the bill was called and discharged by pen with great generosity loike a foin young english gentleman of th olden toime be jove costigan enthusiastically remarked <\s>
<s> and as when they went out of the box he stepped forward and gave mrs <\s>
<s> bolton his arm fanny fell to pen's lot and the young people walked away in high good humour together in the wake of their seniors <\s>
<s> the champagne and the rack punch though taken in moderation by all persons except perhaps poor cos who lurched ever so little in his gait had set them in high spirits and good humour so that fanny began to skip and move her brisk little feet in time to the band which was playing waltzes and galops for the dancers <\s>
<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>
<s> shouldn't you like a turn <\s>
<s> said the prince of fairoaks <\s>
<s> what fun it would be <\s>
<s> bolton ma'am do let me take her once round <\s>
<s> costigan said off wid you <\s>
<s> bolton not refusing indeed she was an old war horse and would have liked at the trumpet's sound to have entered the arena herself fanny's shawl was off her back in a minute and she and arthur were whirling round in a waltz in the midst of a great deal of queer but exceedingly joyful company <\s>
<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>
<s> huxter and his pink satin young friend of whom we have already had a glimpse <\s>
<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>
<s> the young surgeon roared out using at the same time other expressions far more emphatic and was joined in his abuse by the shrill language and laughter of his partner to the interruption of the ball the terror of poor little fanny and the immense indignation of pen <\s>
<s> arthur was furious and not so angry at the quarrel as at the shame attending it <\s>
<s> a battle with a fellow like that <\s>
<s> a row in a public garden and with a porter's daughter on his arm <\s>
<s> what a position for arthur pendennis <\s>
<s> he drew poor little fanny hastily away from the dancers to her mother and wished that lady and costigan and poor fanny underground rather than there in his companionship and under his protection <\s>
<s> when huxter commenced his attack that free spoken young gentleman had not seen who was his opponent and directly he was aware that it was arthur whom he had insulted he began to make apologies <\s>
<s> hold your stoopid tongue mary he said to his partner <\s>
<s> it's an old friend and crony at home <\s>
<s> i beg pardon pendennis wasn't aware it was you old boy <\s>
<s> and he set off running with the rest of the crowd in the direction of the fireworks <\s>
<s> so did pen presently when this agreeable youth was out of sight begin to run with his little companion mrs <\s>
<s> bolton following after them with captain costigan at her side <\s>
<s> but the captain was too majestic and dignified in his movements to run for friend or enemy and he pursued his course with the usual jaunty swagger which distinguished his steps so that he and his companion were speedily distanced by pen and miss fanny <\s>
<s> perhaps arthur forgot or perhaps he did not choose to remember that the elder couple had no money in their pockets as had been proved by their adventure at the entrance of the gardens howbeit pen paid a couple of shillings for himself and his partner and with her hanging close on his arm scaled the staircase which leads to the firework gallery <\s>
<s> the captain and mamma might have followed them if they liked but arthur and fanny were too busy to look back <\s>
<s> people were pushing and squeezing there beside and behind them <\s>
<s> one eager individual rushed by fanny and elbowed her so that she fell back with a little cry upon which of course arthur caught her adroitly in his arms and just for protection kept her so defended until they mounted the stair and took their places <\s>
<s> poor foker sate alone on one of the highest benches his face illuminated by the fireworks or in their absence by the moon <\s>
<s> arthur saw him and laughed but did not occupy himself about his friend much <\s>
<s> he was engaged with fanny <\s>
<s> how happy she was <\s>
<s> how she cried o o o as the rockets soared into the air and showered down in azure and emerald and vermilion <\s>
<s> as these wonders blazed and disappeared before her the little girl thrilled and trembled with delight at arthur's side her hand was under his arm still he felt it pressing him as she looked up delighted <\s>
<s> how beautiful they are sir <\s>
<s> don't call me sir fanny arthur said <\s>
<s> a quick blush rushed up into the girl's face <\s>
<s> what shall i call you <\s>
<s> she said in a low voice sweet and tremulous <\s>
<s> what would you wish me to say sir <\s>
<s> well i forgot it is best so my dear pendennis said very kindly and gently <\s>
<s> i may call you fanny <\s>
<s> she said and the little hand pressed his arm once more very eagerly and the girl clung to him so that he could feel her heart beating on his shoulder <\s>
<s> i may call you fanny because you are a young girl and a good girl fanny and i am an old gentleman <\s>
<s> but you mustn't call me anything but sir or mr <\s>

<s> are you afraid of me <\s>
<s> do you think i would hurt you <\s>
<s> not for all the world my dear little girl <\s>
<s> and and look how beautiful the moon and stars are and how calmly they shine when the rockets have gone out and the noisy wheels have done hissing and blazing <\s>
<s> when i came here to night i did not think i should have had such a pretty little companion to sit by my side and see these fine fireworks <\s>
<s> you must know i live by myself and work very hard <\s>
<s> i write in books and newspapers fanny and i quite tired out and was expected to sit alone all night and don't cry my dear dear little girl <\s>
<s> here pen broke out rapidly putting an end to the calm oration which he had begun to deliver for the sight of a woman's tears always put his nerves in a quiver and he began forthwith to coax her and soothe her and to utter a hundred and twenty little ejaculations of pity and sympathy which need not be repeated here because they would be absurd in print <\s>
<s> so would a mother's talk to a child be absurd in print so would a lover's to his bride <\s>
<s> that sweet artless poetry bears no translation and is too subtle for grammarians clumsy definitions <\s>
<s> you have but the same four letters to describe the salute which you perform on your grandmother's forehead and that which you bestow on the sacred cheek of your mistress but the same four letters and not one of them a labial <\s>
<s> do we mean to hint that r <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis made any use of the monosyllable in question <\s>
<s> in the first place it was dark the fireworks were over and nobody could see him secondly he was not a man to have this kind of secret and tell it thirdly and lastly let the honest fellow who has kissed a pretty girl say what would have been his own conduct in such a delicate juncture <\s>
<s> well the truth is that however you may suspect him and whatever you would have done under the circumstances or mr <\s>
<s> pen would have liked to do he behaved honestly and like a man <\s>
<s> i will not play with this little girl's heart he said within himself and forget my own or her honour <\s>

<s> you must know i live by myself and work very hard <\s>
<s> i write in books and newspapers fanny and i quite tired out and was expected to sit alone all night and don't cry my dear dear little girl <\s>
<s> here pen broke out rapidly putting an end to the calm oration which he had begun to deliver for the sight of a woman's tears always put his nerves in a quiver and he began forthwith to coax her and soothe her and to utter a hundred and twenty little ejaculations of pity and sympathy which need not be repeated here because they would be absurd in print <\s>
<s> so would a mother's talk to a child be absurd in print so would a lover's to his bride <\s>
<s> that sweet artless poetry bears no translation and is too subtle for grammarians clumsy definitions <\s>
<s> you have but the same four letters to describe the salute which you perform on your grandmother's forehead and that which you bestow on the sacred cheek of your mistress but the same four letters and not one of them a labial <\s>
<s> do we mean to hint that r <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis made any use of the monosyllable in question <\s>
<s> in the first place it was dark the fireworks were over and nobody could see him secondly he was not a man to have this kind of secret and tell it thirdly and lastly let the honest fellow who has kissed a pretty girl say what would have been his own conduct in such a delicate juncture <\s>
<s> well the truth is that however you may suspect him and whatever you would have done under the circumstances or mr <\s>
<s> pen would have liked to do he behaved honestly and like a man <\s>
<s> i will not play with this little girl's heart he said within himself and forget my own or her honour <\s>
<s> she seems to have a great deal of dangerous and rather contagious sensibility and i am very glad the fireworks are over and that i can take her back to her mother <\s>

<s> bolton be kind to me and oblige me <\s>
<s> i shan't have the heart to sup without you and upon my word i have had no dinner <\s>

<s> bolton angry with me unless she will favour me with her society <\s>
<s> and we will all sup quietly and go back in a cab together <\s>
<s> the cab the lobster salad the frank and good humoured look of pendennis as he smilingly invited the worthy matron subdued her suspicions and her anger <\s>
<s> since he would be so obliging she thought she could take a little bit of lobster and so they all marched away to a box and costigan called for a waither with such a loud and belligerent voice as caused one of those officials instantly to run to him <\s>
<s> the carte was examined on the wall and fanny was asked to choose her favourite dish upon which the young creature said she was fond of lobster too but also owned to a partiality for raspberry tart <\s>
<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>
<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>
<s> when the supper which was very brisk and gay was over and captain costigan and mrs <\s>
<s> bolton had partaken of some of the rack punch that is so fragrant at vauxhall the bill was called and discharged by pen with great generosity loike a foin young english gentleman of th olden toime be jove costigan enthusiastically remarked <\s>
<s> and as when they went out of the box he stepped forward and gave mrs <\s>
<s> bolton his arm fanny fell to pen's lot and the young people walked away in high good humour together in the wake of their seniors <\s>
<s> the champagne and the rack punch though taken in moderation by all persons except perhaps poor cos who lurched ever so little in his gait had set them in high spirits and good humour so that fanny began to skip and move her brisk little feet in time to the band which was playing waltzes and galops for the dancers <\s>
<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>
<s> shouldn't you like a turn <\s>
<s> said the prince of fairoaks <\s>
<s> what fun it would be <\s>
<s> bolton ma'am do let me take her once round <\s>
<s> costigan said off wid you <\s>
<s> bolton not refusing indeed she was an old war horse and would have liked at the trumpet's sound to have entered the arena herself fanny's shawl was off her back in a minute and she and arthur were whirling round in a waltz in the midst of a great deal of queer but exceedingly joyful company <\s>
<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>
<s> huxter and his pink satin young friend of whom we have already had a glimpse <\s>
<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>
<s> the young surgeon roared out using at the same time other expressions far more emphatic and was joined in his abuse by the shrill language and laughter of his partner to the interruption of the ball the terror of poor little fanny and the immense indignation of pen <\s>
<s> arthur was furious and not so angry at the quarrel as at the shame attending it <\s>
<s> a battle with a fellow like that <\s>
<s> a row in a public garden and with a porter's daughter on his arm <\s>
<s> what a position for arthur pendennis <\s>
<s> he drew poor little fanny hastily away from the dancers to her mother and wished that lady and costigan and poor fanny underground rather than there in his companionship and under his protection <\s>
<s> when huxter commenced his attack that free spoken young gentleman had not seen who was his opponent and directly he was aware that it was arthur whom he had insulted he began to make apologies <\s>

<s> it's an old friend and crony at home <\s>
<s> i beg pardon pendennis wasn't aware it was you old boy <\s>

<s> bolton following after them with captain costigan at her side <\s>
<s> but the captain was too majestic and dignified in his movements to run for friend or enemy and he pursued his course with the usual jaunty swagger which distinguished his steps so that he and his companion were speedily distanced by pen and miss fanny <\s>
<s> perhaps arthur forgot or perhaps he did not choose to remember that the elder couple had no money in their pockets as had been proved by their adventure at the entrance of the gardens howbeit pen paid a couple of shillings for himself and his partner and with her hanging close on his arm scaled the staircase which leads to the firework gallery <\s>
<s> the captain and mamma might have followed them if they liked but arthur and fanny were too busy to look back <\s>

<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>
<s> huxter and his pink satin young friend of whom we have already had a glimpse <\s>
<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>
<s> the young surgeon roared out using at the same time other expressions far more emphatic and was joined in his abuse by the shrill language and laughter of his partner to the interruption of the ball the terror of poor little fanny and the immense indignation of pen <\s>
<s> arthur was furious and not so angry at the quarrel as at the shame attending it <\s>
<s> a battle with a fellow like that <\s>
<s> a row in a public garden and with a porter's daughter on his arm <\s>
<s> what a position for arthur pendennis <\s>

<s> it's an old friend and crony at home <\s>
<s> i beg pardon pendennis wasn't aware it was you old boy <\s>

<s> so did pen presently when this agreeable youth was out of sight begin to run with his little companion mrs <\s>
<s> bolton following after them with captain costigan at her side <\s>
<s> but the captain was too majestic and dignified in his movements to run for friend or enemy and he pursued his course with the usual jaunty swagger which distinguished his steps so that he and his companion were speedily distanced by pen and miss fanny <\s>
<s> perhaps arthur forgot or perhaps he did not choose to remember that the elder couple had no money in their pockets as had been proved by their adventure at the entrance of the gardens howbeit pen paid a couple of shillings for himself and his partner and with her hanging close on his arm scaled the staircase which leads to the firework gallery <\s>
<s> the captain and mamma might have followed them if they liked but arthur and fanny were too busy to look back <\s>
<s> people were pushing and squeezing there beside and behind them <\s>
<s> one eager individual rushed by fanny and elbowed her so that she fell back with a little cry upon which of course arthur caught her adroitly in his arms and just for protection kept her so defended until they mounted the stair and took their places <\s>
<s> poor foker sate alone on one of the highest benches his face illuminated by the fireworks or in their absence by the moon <\s>
<s> arthur saw him and laughed but did not occupy himself about his friend much <\s>
<s> he was engaged with fanny <\s>
<s> how happy she was <\s>
<s> how she cried o o o as the rockets soared into the air and showered down in azure and emerald and vermilion <\s>
<s> as these wonders blazed and disappeared before her the little girl thrilled and trembled with delight at arthur's side her hand was under his arm still he felt it pressing him as she looked up delighted <\s>
<s> how beautiful they are sir <\s>
<s> don't call me sir fanny arthur said <\s>
<s> a quick blush rushed up into the girl's face <\s>
<s> what shall i call you <\s>
<s> she said in a low voice sweet and tremulous <\s>
<s> what would you wish me to say sir <\s>
<s> well i forgot it is best so my dear pendennis said very kindly and gently <\s>
<s> i may call you fanny <\s>
<s> she said and the little hand pressed his arm once more very eagerly and the girl clung to him so that he could feel her heart beating on his shoulder <\s>

<s> but you mustn't call me anything but sir or mr <\s>

<s> are you afraid of me <\s>
<s> do you think i would hurt you <\s>
<s> not for all the world my dear little girl <\s>
<s> and and look how beautiful the moon and stars are and how calmly they shine when the rockets have gone out and the noisy wheels have done hissing and blazing <\s>
<s> when i came here to night i did not think i should have had such a pretty little companion to sit by my side and see these fine fireworks <\s>
<s> you must know i live by myself and work very hard <\s>
<s> i write in books and newspapers fanny and i quite tired out and was expected to sit alone all night and don't cry my dear dear little girl <\s>
<s> here pen broke out rapidly putting an end to the calm oration which he had begun to deliver for the sight of a woman's tears always put his nerves in a quiver and he began forthwith to coax her and soothe her and to utter a hundred and twenty little ejaculations of pity and sympathy which need not be repeated here because they would be absurd in print <\s>
<s> so would a mother's talk to a child be absurd in print so would a lover's to his bride <\s>
<s> that sweet artless poetry bears no translation and is too subtle for grammarians clumsy definitions <\s>
<s> you have but the same four letters to describe the salute which you perform on your grandmother's forehead and that which you bestow on the sacred cheek of your mistress but the same four letters and not one of them a labial <\s>
<s> do we mean to hint that r <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis made any use of the monosyllable in question <\s>
<s> in the first place it was dark the fireworks were over and nobody could see him secondly he was not a man to have this kind of secret and tell it thirdly and lastly let the honest fellow who has kissed a pretty girl say what would have been his own conduct in such a delicate juncture <\s>
<s> well the truth is that however you may suspect him and whatever you would have done under the circumstances or mr <\s>
<s> pen would have liked to do he behaved honestly and like a man <\s>
<s> i will not play with this little girl's heart he said within himself and forget my own or her honour <\s>

<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>

<s> the cab the lobster salad the frank and good humoured look of pendennis as he smilingly invited the worthy matron subdued her suspicions and her anger <\s>
<s> since he would be so obliging she thought she could take a little bit of lobster and so they all marched away to a box and costigan called for a waither with such a loud and belligerent voice as caused one of those officials instantly to run to him <\s>
<s> the carte was examined on the wall and fanny was asked to choose her favourite dish upon which the young creature said she was fond of lobster too but also owned to a partiality for raspberry tart <\s>
<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>
<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>
<s> when the supper which was very brisk and gay was over and captain costigan and mrs <\s>

<s> and as when they went out of the box he stepped forward and gave mrs <\s>
<s> bolton his arm fanny fell to pen's lot and the young people walked away in high good humour together in the wake of their seniors <\s>
<s> the champagne and the rack punch though taken in moderation by all persons except perhaps poor cos who lurched ever so little in his gait had set them in high spirits and good humour so that fanny began to skip and move her brisk little feet in time to the band which was playing waltzes and galops for the dancers <\s>
<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>

<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>
<s> huxter and his pink satin young friend of whom we have already had a glimpse <\s>
<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>
<s> the young surgeon roared out using at the same time other expressions far more emphatic and was joined in his abuse by the shrill language and laughter of his partner to the interruption of the ball the terror of poor little fanny and the immense indignation of pen <\s>

<s> the young surgeon roared out using at the same time other expressions far more emphatic and was joined in his abuse by the shrill language and laughter of his partner to the interruption of the ball the terror of poor little fanny and the immense indignation of pen <\s>

<s> a row in a public garden and with a porter's daughter on his arm <\s>

<s> it's an old friend and crony at home <\s>
<s> i beg pardon pendennis wasn't aware it was you old boy <\s>

<s> bolton following after them with captain costigan at her side <\s>
<s> but the captain was too majestic and dignified in his movements to run for friend or enemy and he pursued his course with the usual jaunty swagger which distinguished his steps so that he and his companion were speedily distanced by pen and miss fanny <\s>
<s> perhaps arthur forgot or perhaps he did not choose to remember that the elder couple had no money in their pockets as had been proved by their adventure at the entrance of the gardens howbeit pen paid a couple of shillings for himself and his partner and with her hanging close on his arm scaled the staircase which leads to the firework gallery <\s>
<s> the captain and mamma might have followed them if they liked but arthur and fanny were too busy to look back <\s>
<s> people were pushing and squeezing there beside and behind them <\s>

<s> poor foker sate alone on one of the highest benches his face illuminated by the fireworks or in their absence by the moon <\s>
<s> arthur saw him and laughed but did not occupy himself about his friend much <\s>
<s> he was engaged with fanny <\s>
<s> how happy she was <\s>

<s> as these wonders blazed and disappeared before her the little girl thrilled and trembled with delight at arthur's side her hand was under his arm still he felt it pressing him as she looked up delighted <\s>
<s> how beautiful they are sir <\s>
<s> don't call me sir fanny arthur said <\s>

<s> she said in a low voice sweet and tremulous <\s>

<s> i may call you fanny <\s>

<s> do you think i would hurt you <\s>

<s> you must know i live by myself and work very hard <\s>
<s> i write in books and newspapers fanny and i quite tired out and was expected to sit alone all night and don't cry my dear dear little girl <\s>
<s> here pen broke out rapidly putting an end to the calm oration which he had begun to deliver for the sight of a woman's tears always put his nerves in a quiver and he began forthwith to coax her and soothe her and to utter a hundred and twenty little ejaculations of pity and sympathy which need not be repeated here because they would be absurd in print <\s>
<s> so would a mother's talk to a child be absurd in print so would a lover's to his bride <\s>

<s> arthur pendennis made any use of the monosyllable in question <\s>

<s> the cab the lobster salad the frank and good humoured look of pendennis as he smilingly invited the worthy matron subdued her suspicions and her anger <\s>
<s> since he would be so obliging she thought she could take a little bit of lobster and so they all marched away to a box and costigan called for a waither with such a loud and belligerent voice as caused one of those officials instantly to run to him <\s>
<s> the carte was examined on the wall and fanny was asked to choose her favourite dish upon which the young creature said she was fond of lobster too but also owned to a partiality for raspberry tart <\s>
<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>
<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>
<s> when the supper which was very brisk and gay was over and captain costigan and mrs <\s>

<s> and as when they went out of the box he stepped forward and gave mrs <\s>
<s> bolton his arm fanny fell to pen's lot and the young people walked away in high good humour together in the wake of their seniors <\s>
<s> the champagne and the rack punch though taken in moderation by all persons except perhaps poor cos who lurched ever so little in his gait had set them in high spirits and good humour so that fanny began to skip and move her brisk little feet in time to the band which was playing waltzes and galops for the dancers <\s>
<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>

<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>
<s> huxter and his pink satin young friend of whom we have already had a glimpse <\s>
<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>
<s> the young surgeon roared out using at the same time other expressions far more emphatic and was joined in his abuse by the shrill language and laughter of his partner to the interruption of the ball the terror of poor little fanny and the immense indignation of pen <\s>
<s> arthur was furious and not so angry at the quarrel as at the shame attending it <\s>
<s> a battle with a fellow like that <\s>

<s> perhaps arthur forgot or perhaps he did not choose to remember that the elder couple had no money in their pockets as had been proved by their adventure at the entrance of the gardens howbeit pen paid a couple of shillings for himself and his partner and with her hanging close on his arm scaled the staircase which leads to the firework gallery <\s>

<s> here pen broke out rapidly putting an end to the calm oration which he had begun to deliver for the sight of a woman's tears always put his nerves in a quiver and he began forthwith to coax her and soothe her and to utter a hundred and twenty little ejaculations of pity and sympathy which need not be repeated here because they would be absurd in print <\s>
<s> so would a mother's talk to a child be absurd in print so would a lover's to his bride <\s>

<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>
<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>

<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>

<s> the cab the lobster salad the frank and good humoured look of pendennis as he smilingly invited the worthy matron subdued her suspicions and her anger <\s>
<s> since he would be so obliging she thought she could take a little bit of lobster and so they all marched away to a box and costigan called for a waither with such a loud and belligerent voice as caused one of those officials instantly to run to him <\s>
<s> the carte was examined on the wall and fanny was asked to choose her favourite dish upon which the young creature said she was fond of lobster too but also owned to a partiality for raspberry tart <\s>
<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>
<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>
<s> when the supper which was very brisk and gay was over and captain costigan and mrs <\s>
<s> bolton had partaken of some of the rack punch that is so fragrant at vauxhall the bill was called and discharged by pen with great generosity loike a foin young english gentleman of th olden toime be jove costigan enthusiastically remarked <\s>
<s> and as when they went out of the box he stepped forward and gave mrs <\s>
<s> bolton his arm fanny fell to pen's lot and the young people walked away in high good humour together in the wake of their seniors <\s>
<s> the champagne and the rack punch though taken in moderation by all persons except perhaps poor cos who lurched ever so little in his gait had set them in high spirits and good humour so that fanny began to skip and move her brisk little feet in time to the band which was playing waltzes and galops for the dancers <\s>
<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>
<s> shouldn't you like a turn <\s>
<s> said the prince of fairoaks <\s>
<s> what fun it would be <\s>
<s> bolton ma'am do let me take her once round <\s>
<s> costigan said off wid you <\s>
<s> bolton not refusing indeed she was an old war horse and would have liked at the trumpet's sound to have entered the arena herself fanny's shawl was off her back in a minute and she and arthur were whirling round in a waltz in the midst of a great deal of queer but exceedingly joyful company <\s>
<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>
<s> huxter and his pink satin young friend of whom we have already had a glimpse <\s>
<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>
<s> the young surgeon roared out using at the same time other expressions far more emphatic and was joined in his abuse by the shrill language and laughter of his partner to the interruption of the ball the terror of poor little fanny and the immense indignation of pen <\s>
<s> arthur was furious and not so angry at the quarrel as at the shame attending it <\s>
<s> a battle with a fellow like that <\s>
<s> a row in a public garden and with a porter's daughter on his arm <\s>
<s> what a position for arthur pendennis <\s>
<s> he drew poor little fanny hastily away from the dancers to her mother and wished that lady and costigan and poor fanny underground rather than there in his companionship and under his protection <\s>
<s> when huxter commenced his attack that free spoken young gentleman had not seen who was his opponent and directly he was aware that it was arthur whom he had insulted he began to make apologies <\s>
<s> hold your stoopid tongue mary he said to his partner <\s>
<s> it's an old friend and crony at home <\s>
<s> i beg pardon pendennis wasn't aware it was you old boy <\s>
<s> and he set off running with the rest of the crowd in the direction of the fireworks <\s>
<s> so did pen presently when this agreeable youth was out of sight begin to run with his little companion mrs <\s>
<s> bolton following after them with captain costigan at her side <\s>
<s> but the captain was too majestic and dignified in his movements to run for friend or enemy and he pursued his course with the usual jaunty swagger which distinguished his steps so that he and his companion were speedily distanced by pen and miss fanny <\s>
<s> perhaps arthur forgot or perhaps he did not choose to remember that the elder couple had no money in their pockets as had been proved by their adventure at the entrance of the gardens howbeit pen paid a couple of shillings for himself and his partner and with her hanging close on his arm scaled the staircase which leads to the firework gallery <\s>
<s> the captain and mamma might have followed them if they liked but arthur and fanny were too busy to look back <\s>
<s> people were pushing and squeezing there beside and behind them <\s>
<s> one eager individual rushed by fanny and elbowed her so that she fell back with a little cry upon which of course arthur caught her adroitly in his arms and just for protection kept her so defended until they mounted the stair and took their places <\s>
<s> poor foker sate alone on one of the highest benches his face illuminated by the fireworks or in their absence by the moon <\s>
<s> arthur saw him and laughed but did not occupy himself about his friend much <\s>
<s> he was engaged with fanny <\s>
<s> how happy she was <\s>
<s> how she cried o o o as the rockets soared into the air and showered down in azure and emerald and vermilion <\s>
<s> as these wonders blazed and disappeared before her the little girl thrilled and trembled with delight at arthur's side her hand was under his arm still he felt it pressing him as she looked up delighted <\s>

<s> here pen broke out rapidly putting an end to the calm oration which he had begun to deliver for the sight of a woman's tears always put his nerves in a quiver and he began forthwith to coax her and soothe her and to utter a hundred and twenty little ejaculations of pity and sympathy which need not be repeated here because they would be absurd in print <\s>
<s> so would a mother's talk to a child be absurd in print so would a lover's to his bride <\s>

<s> here pen broke out rapidly putting an end to the calm oration which he had begun to deliver for the sight of a woman's tears always put his nerves in a quiver and he began forthwith to coax her and soothe her and to utter a hundred and twenty little ejaculations of pity and sympathy which need not be repeated here because they would be absurd in print <\s>

<s> the cab the lobster salad the frank and good humoured look of pendennis as he smilingly invited the worthy matron subdued her suspicions and her anger <\s>
<s> since he would be so obliging she thought she could take a little bit of lobster and so they all marched away to a box and costigan called for a waither with such a loud and belligerent voice as caused one of those officials instantly to run to him <\s>
<s> the carte was examined on the wall and fanny was asked to choose her favourite dish upon which the young creature said she was fond of lobster too but also owned to a partiality for raspberry tart <\s>
<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>
<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>
<s> when the supper which was very brisk and gay was over and captain costigan and mrs <\s>
<s> bolton had partaken of some of the rack punch that is so fragrant at vauxhall the bill was called and discharged by pen with great generosity loike a foin young english gentleman of th olden toime be jove costigan enthusiastically remarked <\s>
<s> and as when they went out of the box he stepped forward and gave mrs <\s>
<s> bolton his arm fanny fell to pen's lot and the young people walked away in high good humour together in the wake of their seniors <\s>
<s> the champagne and the rack punch though taken in moderation by all persons except perhaps poor cos who lurched ever so little in his gait had set them in high spirits and good humour so that fanny began to skip and move her brisk little feet in time to the band which was playing waltzes and galops for the dancers <\s>
<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>

<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>

<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>

<s> the carte was examined on the wall and fanny was asked to choose her favourite dish upon which the young creature said she was fond of lobster too but also owned to a partiality for raspberry tart <\s>
<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>
<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>
<s> when the supper which was very brisk and gay was over and captain costigan and mrs <\s>
<s> bolton had partaken of some of the rack punch that is so fragrant at vauxhall the bill was called and discharged by pen with great generosity loike a foin young english gentleman of th olden toime be jove costigan enthusiastically remarked <\s>
<s> and as when they went out of the box he stepped forward and gave mrs <\s>
<s> bolton his arm fanny fell to pen's lot and the young people walked away in high good humour together in the wake of their seniors <\s>
<s> the champagne and the rack punch though taken in moderation by all persons except perhaps poor cos who lurched ever so little in his gait had set them in high spirits and good humour so that fanny began to skip and move her brisk little feet in time to the band which was playing waltzes and galops for the dancers <\s>
<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>
<s> shouldn't you like a turn <\s>
<s> said the prince of fairoaks <\s>
<s> what fun it would be <\s>
<s> bolton ma'am do let me take her once round <\s>
<s> costigan said off wid you <\s>
<s> bolton not refusing indeed she was an old war horse and would have liked at the trumpet's sound to have entered the arena herself fanny's shawl was off her back in a minute and she and arthur were whirling round in a waltz in the midst of a great deal of queer but exceedingly joyful company <\s>
<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>
<s> huxter and his pink satin young friend of whom we have already had a glimpse <\s>
<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>
<s> the young surgeon roared out using at the same time other expressions far more emphatic and was joined in his abuse by the shrill language and laughter of his partner to the interruption of the ball the terror of poor little fanny and the immense indignation of pen <\s>
<s> arthur was furious and not so angry at the quarrel as at the shame attending it <\s>
<s> a battle with a fellow like that <\s>
<s> a row in a public garden and with a porter's daughter on his arm <\s>
<s> what a position for arthur pendennis <\s>
<s> he drew poor little fanny hastily away from the dancers to her mother and wished that lady and costigan and poor fanny underground rather than there in his companionship and under his protection <\s>
<s> when huxter commenced his attack that free spoken young gentleman had not seen who was his opponent and directly he was aware that it was arthur whom he had insulted he began to make apologies <\s>
<s> hold your stoopid tongue mary he said to his partner <\s>
<s> it's an old friend and crony at home <\s>
<s> i beg pardon pendennis wasn't aware it was you old boy <\s>
<s> and he set off running with the rest of the crowd in the direction of the fireworks <\s>
<s> so did pen presently when this agreeable youth was out of sight begin to run with his little companion mrs <\s>
<s> bolton following after them with captain costigan at her side <\s>
<s> but the captain was too majestic and dignified in his movements to run for friend or enemy and he pursued his course with the usual jaunty swagger which distinguished his steps so that he and his companion were speedily distanced by pen and miss fanny <\s>
<s> perhaps arthur forgot or perhaps he did not choose to remember that the elder couple had no money in their pockets as had been proved by their adventure at the entrance of the gardens howbeit pen paid a couple of shillings for himself and his partner and with her hanging close on his arm scaled the staircase which leads to the firework gallery <\s>
<s> the captain and mamma might have followed them if they liked but arthur and fanny were too busy to look back <\s>
<s> people were pushing and squeezing there beside and behind them <\s>
<s> one eager individual rushed by fanny and elbowed her so that she fell back with a little cry upon which of course arthur caught her adroitly in his arms and just for protection kept her so defended until they mounted the stair and took their places <\s>
<s> poor foker sate alone on one of the highest benches his face illuminated by the fireworks or in their absence by the moon <\s>
<s> arthur saw him and laughed but did not occupy himself about his friend much <\s>
<s> he was engaged with fanny <\s>
<s> how happy she was <\s>
<s> how she cried o o o as the rockets soared into the air and showered down in azure and emerald and vermilion <\s>
<s> as these wonders blazed and disappeared before her the little girl thrilled and trembled with delight at arthur's side her hand was under his arm still he felt it pressing him as she looked up delighted <\s>
<s> how beautiful they are sir <\s>
<s> don't call me sir fanny arthur said <\s>
<s> a quick blush rushed up into the girl's face <\s>

<s> she said in a low voice sweet and tremulous <\s>
<s> what would you wish me to say sir <\s>

<s> i may call you fanny <\s>
<s> she said and the little hand pressed his arm once more very eagerly and the girl clung to him so that he could feel her heart beating on his shoulder <\s>

<s> do you think i would hurt you <\s>
<s> not for all the world my dear little girl <\s>

<s> you must know i live by myself and work very hard <\s>
<s> i write in books and newspapers fanny and i quite tired out and was expected to sit alone all night and don't cry my dear dear little girl <\s>
<s> here pen broke out rapidly putting an end to the calm oration which he had begun to deliver for the sight of a woman's tears always put his nerves in a quiver and he began forthwith to coax her and soothe her and to utter a hundred and twenty little ejaculations of pity and sympathy which need not be repeated here because they would be absurd in print <\s>
<s> so would a mother's talk to a child be absurd in print so would a lover's to his bride <\s>
<s> that sweet artless poetry bears no translation and is too subtle for grammarians clumsy definitions <\s>

<s> when i came here to night i did not think i should have had such a pretty little companion to sit by my side and see these fine fireworks <\s>
<s> you must know i live by myself and work very hard <\s>
<s> i write in books and newspapers fanny and i quite tired out and was expected to sit alone all night and don't cry my dear dear little girl <\s>
<s> here pen broke out rapidly putting an end to the calm oration which he had begun to deliver for the sight of a woman's tears always put his nerves in a quiver and he began forthwith to coax her and soothe her and to utter a hundred and twenty little ejaculations of pity and sympathy which need not be repeated here because they would be absurd in print <\s>
<s> so would a mother's talk to a child be absurd in print so would a lover's to his bride <\s>
<s> that sweet artless poetry bears no translation and is too subtle for grammarians clumsy definitions <\s>
<s> you have but the same four letters to describe the salute which you perform on your grandmother's forehead and that which you bestow on the sacred cheek of your mistress but the same four letters and not one of them a labial <\s>
<s> do we mean to hint that r <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis made any use of the monosyllable in question <\s>
<s> in the first place it was dark the fireworks were over and nobody could see him secondly he was not a man to have this kind of secret and tell it thirdly and lastly let the honest fellow who has kissed a pretty girl say what would have been his own conduct in such a delicate juncture <\s>
<s> well the truth is that however you may suspect him and whatever you would have done under the circumstances or mr <\s>
<s> pen would have liked to do he behaved honestly and like a man <\s>
<s> i will not play with this little girl's heart he said within himself and forget my own or her honour <\s>
<s> she seems to have a great deal of dangerous and rather contagious sensibility and i am very glad the fireworks are over and that i can take her back to her mother <\s>

<s> don't stumble you heedless little thing this is the way and there is your mamma at the door <\s>

<s> bolton was unquiet in spirit and grasping her umbrella <\s>

<s> it was so much so that pen could not refrain from bursting into a laugh <\s>

<s> a lobster salad is the best thing in the world for a headache pen said gallantly and a glass of wine i'm sure will do you good <\s>
<s> bolton be kind to me and oblige me <\s>

<s> costigan i'm sure you'll take care of miss fanny and i shall think mrs <\s>
<s> bolton angry with me unless she will favour me with her society <\s>
<s> and we will all sup quietly and go back in a cab together <\s>
<s> the cab the lobster salad the frank and good humoured look of pendennis as he smilingly invited the worthy matron subdued her suspicions and her anger <\s>
<s> since he would be so obliging she thought she could take a little bit of lobster and so they all marched away to a box and costigan called for a waither with such a loud and belligerent voice as caused one of those officials instantly to run to him <\s>
<s> the carte was examined on the wall and fanny was asked to choose her favourite dish upon which the young creature said she was fond of lobster too but also owned to a partiality for raspberry tart <\s>
<s> this delicacy was provided by pen and a bottle of the most frisky champagne was moreover ordered for the delight of the ladies <\s>
<s> little fanny drank this what other sweet intoxication had she not drunk in the course of the night <\s>
<s> when the supper which was very brisk and gay was over and captain costigan and mrs <\s>
<s> bolton had partaken of some of the rack punch that is so fragrant at vauxhall the bill was called and discharged by pen with great generosity loike a foin young english gentleman of th olden toime be jove costigan enthusiastically remarked <\s>
<s> and as when they went out of the box he stepped forward and gave mrs <\s>
<s> bolton his arm fanny fell to pen's lot and the young people walked away in high good humour together in the wake of their seniors <\s>
<s> the champagne and the rack punch though taken in moderation by all persons except perhaps poor cos who lurched ever so little in his gait had set them in high spirits and good humour so that fanny began to skip and move her brisk little feet in time to the band which was playing waltzes and galops for the dancers <\s>
<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>
<s> shouldn't you like a turn <\s>
<s> said the prince of fairoaks <\s>
<s> what fun it would be <\s>
<s> bolton ma'am do let me take her once round <\s>
<s> costigan said off wid you <\s>
<s> bolton not refusing indeed she was an old war horse and would have liked at the trumpet's sound to have entered the arena herself fanny's shawl was off her back in a minute and she and arthur were whirling round in a waltz in the midst of a great deal of queer but exceedingly joyful company <\s>
<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>
<s> huxter and his pink satin young friend of whom we have already had a glimpse <\s>
<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>
<s> the young surgeon roared out using at the same time other expressions far more emphatic and was joined in his abuse by the shrill language and laughter of his partner to the interruption of the ball the terror of poor little fanny and the immense indignation of pen <\s>
<s> arthur was furious and not so angry at the quarrel as at the shame attending it <\s>
<s> a battle with a fellow like that <\s>
<s> a row in a public garden and with a porter's daughter on his arm <\s>
<s> what a position for arthur pendennis <\s>
<s> he drew poor little fanny hastily away from the dancers to her mother and wished that lady and costigan and poor fanny underground rather than there in his companionship and under his protection <\s>
<s> when huxter commenced his attack that free spoken young gentleman had not seen who was his opponent and directly he was aware that it was arthur whom he had insulted he began to make apologies <\s>

<s> it's an old friend and crony at home <\s>
<s> i beg pardon pendennis wasn't aware it was you old boy <\s>

<s> bolton following after them with captain costigan at her side <\s>
<s> but the captain was too majestic and dignified in his movements to run for friend or enemy and he pursued his course with the usual jaunty swagger which distinguished his steps so that he and his companion were speedily distanced by pen and miss fanny <\s>
<s> perhaps arthur forgot or perhaps he did not choose to remember that the elder couple had no money in their pockets as had been proved by their adventure at the entrance of the gardens howbeit pen paid a couple of shillings for himself and his partner and with her hanging close on his arm scaled the staircase which leads to the firework gallery <\s>

<s> as they came up to the dancing the music and fanny's feet seemed to go quicker together she seemed to spring as if naturally from the ground and as if she required repression to keep her there <\s>
<s> shouldn't you like a turn <\s>
<s> said the prince of fairoaks <\s>
<s> what fun it would be <\s>
<s> bolton ma'am do let me take her once round <\s>
<s> costigan said off wid you <\s>
<s> bolton not refusing indeed she was an old war horse and would have liked at the trumpet's sound to have entered the arena herself fanny's shawl was off her back in a minute and she and arthur were whirling round in a waltz in the midst of a great deal of queer but exceedingly joyful company <\s>
<s> pen had no mishap this time with little fanny as he had with miss blanche in old days at least there was no mishap of his making <\s>
<s> the pair danced away with great agility and contentment first a waltz then a galop then a waltz again until in the second waltz they were bumped by another couple who had joined the terpsichorean choir <\s>
<s> huxter and his pink satin young friend of whom we have already had a glimpse <\s>
<s> huxter very probably had been also partaking of supper for he was even more excited now than at the time when he had previously claimed pen's acquaintance and having run against arthur and his partner and nearly knocked them down this amiable gentleman of course began to abuse the people whom he had injured and broke out into a volley of slang against the unoffending couple <\s>
<s> don't keep the ground if you can't dance old slow coach <\s>
<s> the young surgeon roared out using at the same time other expressions far more emphatic and was joined in his abuse by the shrill language and laughter of his partner to the interruption of the ball the terror of poor little fanny and the immense indignation of pen <\s>
<s> arthur was furious and not so angry at the quarrel as at the shame attending it <\s>
<s> a battle with a fellow like that <\s>
<s> a row in a public garden and with a porter's daughter on his arm <\s>
<s> what a position for arthur pendennis <\s>
<s> he drew poor little fanny hastily away from the dancers to her mother and wished that lady and costigan and poor fanny underground rather than there in his companionship and under his protection <\s>
<s> when huxter commenced his attack that free spoken young gentleman had not seen who was his opponent and directly he was aware that it was arthur whom he had insulted he began to make apologies <\s>
<s> hold your stoopid tongue mary he said to his partner <\s>
<s> it's an old friend and crony at home <\s>
<s> i beg pardon pendennis wasn't aware it was you old boy <\s>
<s> and he set off running with the rest of the crowd in the direction of the fireworks <\s>
<s> so did pen presently when this agreeable youth was out of sight begin to run with his little companion mrs <\s>
<s> bolton following after them with captain costigan at her side <\s>
<s> but the captain was too majestic and dignified in his movements to run for friend or enemy and he pursued his course with the usual jaunty swagger which distinguished his steps so that he and his companion were speedily distanced by pen and miss fanny <\s>
<s> perhaps arthur forgot or perhaps he did not choose to remember that the elder couple had no money in their pockets as had been proved by their adventure at the entrance of the gardens howbeit pen paid a couple of shillings for himself and his partner and with her hanging close on his arm scaled the staircase which leads to the firework gallery <\s>
<s> the captain and mamma might have followed them if they liked but arthur and fanny were too busy to look back <\s>
<s> people were pushing and squeezing there beside and behind them <\s>
<s> one eager individual rushed by fanny and elbowed her so that she fell back with a little cry upon which of course arthur caught her adroitly in his arms and just for protection kept her so defended until they mounted the stair and took their places <\s>
<s> poor foker sate alone on one of the highest benches his face illuminated by the fireworks or in their absence by the moon <\s>
<s> arthur saw him and laughed but did not occupy himself about his friend much <\s>
<s> he was engaged with fanny <\s>
<s> how happy she was <\s>
<s> how she cried o o o as the rockets soared into the air and showered down in azure and emerald and vermilion <\s>
<s> as these wonders blazed and disappeared before her the little girl thrilled and trembled with delight at arthur's side her hand was under his arm still he felt it pressing him as she looked up delighted <\s>
<s> how beautiful they are sir <\s>
<s> don't call me sir fanny arthur said <\s>
<s> a quick blush rushed up into the girl's face <\s>

<s> she said in a low voice sweet and tremulous <\s>
